1942 Disassembly (NES)

This is a machine-generated disassembly, not a hand-curated reverse engineering. Code reachable from the RESET / NMI / IRQ vectors is decoded as 6502 instructions; everything else is shown as raw .byte data. Routines are auto-labeled L_xxxx at every JSR/JMP/branch target and data references are labeled D_xxxx. NES hardware registers (PPUCTRL, OAMDMA, etc.) and the small RAM map documented at Data Crystal (score, lives, rolls, level) are resolved by name.

The ROM is NROM-256 (mapper 0): 32 KB PRG mapped at $8000-$ffff plus 8 KB CHR. Only the PRG is disassembled here.

Game Genie codes (from gamegenie.com): IESUTYZA/AESUTYZE set 1P starting lives to 6/9; IAKUUAZA/AAKUUAZE set P1 continue lives in 2P; IASUOAZA/AASUOAZE set P2 lives; PASIOALE sets both players to 9 rolls. The patch sites these target appear in the listing below as STA Lives_Ones / STA Rolls stores after game start.

********************************************************************************
* 1942 (NES) — Capcom, December 1985                                           *
* iNES: PRG=2x16K  CHR=1x8K  mapper=0  flags6=$00  flags7=$08                  *
* Vectors: NMI=$c030  RESET=$bf90  IRQ=$bf90                                   *
********************************************************************************

; ----- NES hardware registers -----
PPUCTRL      = $2000
PPUMASK      = $2001
PPUSTATUS    = $2002
OAMADDR      = $2003
OAMDATA      = $2004
PPUSCROLL    = $2005
PPUADDR      = $2006
PPUDATA      = $2007
SQ1_VOL      = $4000
SQ1_SWEEP    = $4001
SQ1_LO       = $4002
SQ1_HI       = $4003
SQ2_VOL      = $4004
SQ2_SWEEP    = $4005
SQ2_LO       = $4006
SQ2_HI       = $4007
TRI_LINEAR   = $4008
TRI_LO       = $400a
TRI_HI       = $400b
NOISE_VOL    = $400c
NOISE_LO     = $400e
NOISE_HI     = $400f
DMC_FREQ     = $4010
DMC_RAW      = $4011
DMC_START    = $4012
DMC_LEN      = $4013
OAMDMA       = $4014
SND_CHN      = $4015
JOY1         = $4016
JOY2         = $4017

; ----- 1942 RAM map (Data Crystal + discoveries) -----
VBlank_Counter = $0062  ; incremented at $c106 in the NMI tail; Main_Loop at $c2e8 spins until it reaches 3, then resets it. Effectively gates the game to one logic step per 3 VBlanks (~20 Hz)
NMI_SaveA    = $0063  ; NMI prologue stash for the A register (restored by the NMI epilogue before RTI)
NMI_SaveY    = $0065  ; NMI prologue stash for the Y register
PPU_WriteCount = $0087  ; byte count consumed by PPU_WriteBlock ($801b); 58 write sites across PPU-update code
PPU_AddrLo   = $0088  ; low byte of PPU destination address ($2006 target) used by PPU_WriteBlock
PPU_AddrHi   = $0089  ; high byte of PPU destination address; $89:$88 is the full $2006 word
PPU_SrcLo    = $008a  ; low byte of source pointer read by PPU_WriteBlock at STA $2007; zero-page ($8a),Y fetch
PPU_SrcHi    = $008b  ; high byte of source pointer ($8b:$8a) used by PPU_WriteBlock
PPUCTRL_Shadow = $008c  ; mirror of last value written to $2000; flipping bit $80 gates NMI and is reapplied across routines
PPU_ScrollX  = $008f  ; X-scroll shadow written to PPUSCROLL at $c0e7 each NMI tail. Sourced at $80b3 from $039f (mirror in 33-byte player state); also zeroed by level-reset paths at $bcf9 and $bfea
PPU_ScrollY  = $0090  ; Y-scroll shadow written to PPUSCROLL at $c0ec each NMI tail (the second of the two PPUSCROLL writes that latch X then Y). Sourced at $80b3 from $03a0; cleared by level-reset paths at $bcfb and $bfef. Static during long_idle scenario — the auto-scroll only advances once gameplay action begins
Joypad1_State = $0098  ; P1 controller raw state this frame (8 bits) populated by Joypad_PollOne for X=0
Joypad1_NewPress = $0099  ; P1 controller newly-pressed bits this frame (rising edges of Joypad1_State)
Joypad2_State = $009a  ; P2 controller raw state this frame (populated by Joypad_PollOne for X=1)
Joypad2_NewPress = $009b  ; P2 controller newly-pressed bits this frame
SpawnTable_PtrLo = $00d4  ; low byte of a 16-bit pointer ($d4:$d5) into the active stage's enemy-spawn script. Initialized at $d97b from StageSpawnPtr_Table[NametableSelect>>1]. Advanced by 3 each spawn record at $d9a4 / $da76 (matches the 3-byte spawn-record stride elsewhere). Confirmed via die_once drift: monotonic UP across an in-game run, walking through the stage script
SpawnTable_PtrHi = $00d5  ; high byte of the 16-bit spawn-script pointer; carries the +0 add when SpawnTable_PtrLo overflows at $d9aa / $da7c
Fire_HoldCounter = $00db  ; frames the B (Fire) button has been held; Fire_Handler (L_d2aa) increments while held and rolls over at 10 to call Spawn_Bullet — that's the auto-fire repeat rate (~10 frames between bullets when B is held)
Dives        = $022d  ; loop/dive counter for the player. Game Genie 022D:03 (Infinite Dives) pins this to $03, so the player can always loop. Companion to Rolls ($0436) — the two together are 1942's twin defensive moves
TitleMenu_CursorMask = $032a  ; 5 bytes ($032a-$032e) holding the title-menu cursor sprite mask. The blink loop at $b74e-b75a does `ldy #$04 / lda $032a,Y / eor #$ff / sta $032a,Y / dey / bpl` every (TitleMenu_FrameTimer & 3)==0, so the mask flips between two states roughly every 4 frames. Confirmed via idle_titlescreen drift: all 5 bytes FLIP between $00 and $ff in lockstep
MenuCursor_Latched = $0381  ; mode chosen on the title screen, latched in by START at $b771 via `lda MenuCursor_Index / sta $0381`. Read by the game-init paths to pick the 1P/2P scenario
Select_Debounce = $0382  ; title-screen SELECT-held debounce flag: nonzero means SELECT was held last frame. Set to $ff at $b6d5 on the rising edge so the cursor only advances once per press; cleared at $b717 when SELECT is released
P2_Active    = $0384  ; companion to P1_Active; tested by P1_LifeLost at $b80a to decide whether to swap players or game-over
P1_Active    = $0385  ; $ff while P1 is the active player; cleared on game-over. Set at $b7da during NewGame_Init_P1
Active_Player_Index = $0386  ; 0 = P1 currently playing, 1 = P2 currently playing. NewGame_Init_P1 inits to 0; SwapTo_P2 sets to 1, SwapTo_P1 / Restore_P1_NoSave set to 0
Button_DebounceFlags = $0388  ; per-button 'held last frame' flags consumed by the input dispatchers. bit $10 = B (Fire), set/cleared by Fire_Handler ($d2aa); bit $01 = A (Roll), set/cleared by Roll_Handler at $d214. Each handler does a rising-edge detect against its own bit
ScrollY_Target = $03a0  ; persistent Y-scroll source in the active player state block. Copied into $0090 each NMI tail at $80b3, then latched into PPUSCROLL
NametableSelect = $03a1  ; low bit drives PPUCTRL bit 1 (nametable X) at $80b8 — the horizontal scroll-wrap selector. ASL/AND #$02 pattern means bit 0 of this byte toggles which nametable is mapped
PPU_QueueReady = $03ae  ; nonzero -> NMI_Handler walks the PPU_UpdateQueue. NMI clears it on completion ($c07e); set by the queue builder at $81e2
Player_OAM_Y = $03af  ; shadow-OAM mirror of Entity_Y[0] (player)
Player_OAM_X = $03b2  ; shadow-OAM mirror of Entity_X[0] (player), written via DMA
ActivePlayer_State = $0427  ; start of the 33-byte ($21) block holding the currently playing player's state. First 5 bytes ($0427..$042b) are the HUD-display score (BCD digits, low-to-high) — Game Genie 0427:00..042B:00 collectively zero the visible score. Block also holds Lives ($0432), Rolls ($0436), Level, etc.; swapped via SwapTo_P1 / SwapTo_P2 in 2P games. The canonical (true) score lives separately at TrueScore_Lo ($07bf)
Score_D4     = $0428  ; score digit (10,000s)
Score_D3     = $0429  ; score digit (1,000s)
Score_D2     = $042a  ; score digit (100s)
Score_D1     = $042b  ; score digit (10s)
Score_D0     = $042c  ; score digit (1s)
ExtraLife_PendingFlag = $042e  ; set to $ff at $ac7e once the score crosses an extra-life threshold; a nonzero value suppresses re-checking the threshold (the bne $ac8e bypass at $ac72) so each crossing only awards one life. Cleared on game-init
ExtraLife_NextThresh_Hi = $042f  ; high BCD digit of the running 'next extra-life' threshold. Bumped at $acbd via `lda $042f / clc / adc #$01` after each extra life is awarded — combined with the +8 carry into ExtraLife_NextThresh_Lo this raises the next threshold by 80,000 points
ExtraLife_NextThresh_Lo = $0430  ; low BCD digit of the next-extra-life threshold; cleared by the threshold trigger at $ac85 then BCD-incremented by 8 at $acad each award (40 -> 48 wraps to 50, etc.). The first threshold (Score_D4 >= 2 -> 200,000) is hardcoded at $ac74 — these counters only steer subsequent extra lives
Lives_Tens   = $0431  ; lives tens digit
Lives_Ones   = $0432  ; lives ones digit (starts at 02)
Rolls        = $0436  ; special rolls remaining (starts at 03)
Respawn_Count = $0437  ; INC at L_e1e0 each time the player respawns; cleared to 0 by NewGame_Init paths and by debe (post-game-over re-init). Confirmed live: across a 5-death autofire run this byte went 0,0,1,1,2,3,3,4,5 (one increment per death). Tested at >10 sites as a 'have we died yet?' flag (e.g. d09a, d68b — those branches just want nonzero, not the count)
Level        = $0438  ; current stage (00 = stage 1)
Spawn_TallyAlt_Lo = $0439  ; low byte of a parallel 16-bit tally incremented at $ee5f in the same code as Spawn_Tally_Lo (two counters bumped together at every spawn). Likely a per-life or per-stage spawn count vs. the $043d running total
Spawn_TallyAlt_Hi = $043a  ; high byte of the parallel spawn tally; incremented at $ee64 when Spawn_TallyAlt_Lo wraps
Spawn_Tally_Lo = $043d  ; low byte of a 16-bit running tally incremented at $ee67 (right after the entity-spawn site that does `lda #$88 / sta Entity_Active,X`). Carries into Spawn_Tally_Hi via `bne / inc $043e`. Drift confirms ~1 increment per spawn during idle gameplay
Spawn_Tally_Hi = $043e  ; high byte of the 16-bit spawn tally; incremented at $ee6c when Spawn_Tally_Lo wraps
P1_SavedState = $044a  ; 33-byte ($21) save buffer for P1 state while P2 is playing. SwapTo_P2 saves the active block here; SwapTo_P1 / Restore_P1_NoSave load it back into ActivePlayer_State
P2_SavedState = $046b  ; 33-byte ($21) save buffer for P2 state while P1 is playing. SwapTo_P1 saves the active block here; SwapTo_P2 loads it back into ActivePlayer_State
PrevDirection_Save = $048d  ; one-frame stash of the previous Entity_Direction. Written by SetEntityDirection ($d593) before it overwrites $050b,X — lets downstream code detect a direction change
Entity_Active = $048e  ; entity SOA attribute 0 (active flag): bit $80 = slot in use, tested by L_f7cd. The whole entity table is 25 attributes x 25 slots, $19-byte stride per attribute, running $048e..$0682. Slot 0 is the player; Reset_Rolls clears slots 0-11 (player + co-active aux entities)
Entity_Y     = $04a7  ; entity SOA attribute 1 (vertical position); 25 slots at +0..+24 within the table. Slot 0 is the player: UP drives toward $56 (top), DOWN toward $c1 (bottom)
MenuCursor_Y = $04b2  ; Y position of the title-screen menu cursor — physically slot 11 of Entity_Y (the bullet slot during gameplay), repurposed on the title screen. Set to $7f / $8f / $9f for the three menu rows by the dispatch arms at $b6fc / $b702 / $b70a
Entity_X     = $04c0  ; entity SOA attribute 2 (horizontal position); 25 slots. Slot 0 is the player: LEFT drives toward $1e (left edge), RIGHT toward $e6 (right edge). L_aa61 reads Entity_X,X / Entity_X,Y for collision checks between two arbitrary slots
Entity_Direction = $050b  ; entity SOA attribute 5 (8-direction code, $0..$e in steps of 2): $00=UP, $02=UP+RIGHT, $04=RIGHT, $06=DOWN+RIGHT, $08=DOWN, $0a=DOWN+LEFT, $0c=LEFT, $0e=UP+LEFT. Set by SetEntityDirection from the dpad handler. Confirmed live: move_left puts $0c into $050b
Entity_PosY_HiBit = $0524  ; entity SOA attribute 6: high bit of the 24-bit fixed-point Y position. Updated in the Y-position integration at $b061-b08c where the carry from `lda $0399 / adc $0524,X` propagates back via `and #$01 / sta $0524,X`. Slot 0 = player. Pairs with Entity_PosY_FracMid ($053d, attr 7) and Entity_PosY_FracLo ($0556, attr 8) and the displayed integer Entity_Y ($04a7, attr 1)
Entity_PosY_FracMid = $053d  ; entity SOA attribute 7: middle byte of the 24-bit Y position. The physics-tick at $b055-b05b reads `$039a` (Y-velocity mid) and adds it: `lda $039a / adc $053d,X / sta $053d,X`. Carries up into Entity_PosY_HiBit. Confirmed live: copied during slot-clone at $b1ab
Entity_PosY_FracLo = $0556  ; entity SOA attribute 8: lowest sub-pixel byte of the Y position. The physics-tick at $b04c-b052 adds `$039b` (Y-velocity low) into it: `lda $039b / adc $0556,X / sta $0556,X`. Carries into Entity_PosY_FracMid. Confirmed live: copied during slot-clone at $b1a5
Entity_PosX_HiBit = $056f  ; entity SOA attribute 9: high bit of the 24-bit X position. Updated at $b0a2-b0aa where `lda $0396 / adc $056f,X / and #$01 / sta $056f,X` propagates the X-add carry. Pairs with Entity_PosX_FracMid ($0588, attr 10), Entity_PosX_FracLo ($05a1, attr 11), and displayed integer Entity_X ($04c0, attr 2)
Entity_PosX_FracMid = $0588  ; entity SOA attribute 10: middle byte of the 24-bit X position. The physics-tick at $b099-b09f does `lda $0397 / adc $0588,X / sta $0588,X` (adds X-velocity mid byte). Carries up into Entity_PosX_HiBit. Confirmed live: copied during slot-clone at $b1bf, also written at the bullet-init site $d080
Entity_PosX_FracLo = $05a1  ; entity SOA attribute 11: lowest sub-pixel byte of the X position. The physics-tick at $b08f-b096 does `lda $0398 / clc / adc $05a1,X / sta $05a1,X` (adds X-velocity low byte). Carries into Entity_PosX_FracMid. Confirmed live: copied during slot-clone at $b1b9, cleared at the bullet-init site $d088
Entity_TypeId = $05d3  ; entity SOA attribute 13: per-slot enemy/entity type id. Read at $ee79 by EnemyType_DispatchInit which `asl A / tay / lda $eff2,Y / sta PPU_SrcLo / iny / lda $eff2,Y / sta PPU_SrcHi / jmp ($008a)` — i.e. uses the type as an index into the 16-bit pointer table EnemyType_InitDispatch ($eff2) and dispatches to the matching per-type init routine. Confirmed live: enemy_observe drift saw values 03 and 0a appear in slots 14/18/19/20 right after spawns; type 10 ($0a) maps to dispatch entry $ef49
Entity_SpawnTypeRaw = $06cd  ; entity SOA attribute 23: per-slot raw enemy-type id as written by the spawn-script reader at $da3b-$da4d (which fills four consecutive slots Y..Y+3 from scratchpad bytes $b1/$b2/$b2/$b3 — a 4-enemy formation packet). Later copied into Entity_TypeId at $dadf when the slot is activated by Entity_ActivateFromSpawnTable. Survives EntityClear_Slot resets — that's why it's in the persistent-attrs band (4, 13, 19-24)
TitleMenu_FrameTimer = $070b  ; title-screen frame counter for the menu-cursor blink: initialized to $ff at $b6c0 just before the menu loop entry, decremented every iteration at $b744. When (timer & 3)==0 the loop falls through to the cursor-blink eor at $b74e-b75a (the 5-byte mask at TitleMenu_CursorMask). Confirmed via idle_titlescreen drift: SAW with constant -50 step over 150-frame chunks (consistent with one dec per frame, modulo wrap)
Bullet_SpawnPending = $0719  ; $01 written by Spawn_Bullet alongside Bullet_TargetSlot — likely a one-shot 'spawn requested' flag consumed by the entity update pass
Bullet_TargetSlot = $071a  ; $0b written by Spawn_Bullet — the entity slot index ($0b = 11) where the new bullet is being installed. Read at L_d3c3 to look up Entity_Active,Y
Spawn_PatternIndex = $071f  ; 8-state rotating index used by the enemy-spawn routine. Read at $f054 / $f176 / $f34c / $f42c (each masks `and #$07`, ASLs twice to get a 4-byte stride, indexes the spawn-parameter table at $f12e to fetch four per-spawn fields), then incremented in place. Drives wave-pattern variety
HUD_BlinkSubcount = $0725  ; frames-of-current-second for the HUD blink driver: incremented every NMI at $c136 (after the entity-decay loop and SP restore), reset to 0 when it hits $3c (60). Only ticks when P1_Active is set
HUD_BlinkSeconds = $0726  ; seconds counter for the HUD blink driver: incremented at $c145 each time HUD_BlinkSubcount wraps. Bit 0 selects between two 12-byte HUD glyph blocks ($c372 vs $c366) that get copied to OAM at $0200, producing the 1Hz on/off blink (PUSH START / 1UP-style indicator). Confirmed by long_idle drift: +1 per ~1 sec of in-game time
Buttons_Held = $0785  ; current-frame joypad state stored MSB-first (A=$80, B=$40, SEL=$20, START=$10, UP=$08, DOWN=$04, LEFT=$02, RIGHT=$01). NOTE: bit ordering is the OPPOSITE of $98/$9a (which are LSB-first from Joypad_PollOne) — this byte is filled elsewhere in the input stack. Fire_Handler tests bit $40 (B); the input handlers at L_d472 / L_dc54 consume this same byte
PPU_UpdateQueue = $078f  ; variable-length PPU update queue consumed by NMI_Handler. Each entry: addr_hi, addr_lo, count, count×data_byte; queue terminates when count == 0
MenuCursor_Index = $07bb  ; title-screen menu cursor (0=1P normal, 1=1P alt, 2=2P, masked to 0..3). Incremented on each SELECT rising edge at $b6dd; the value drives MenuCursor_Y at $04b2 and TwoPlayer_Mode at $07bc. When the player commits with START, $b771 copies this byte to $0381 as the chosen-mode latch
TwoPlayer_Mode = $07bc  ; 0 = 1P game, nonzero = 2P; set in L_b6da/L_b6f7 from menu choice, gates 2P paths in Continue_Init_P1 / NewGame_Init_P2
WarmBoot_Magic1 = $07bd  ; first half of the warm-boot magic word; Reset_Handler skips RAM-clear when $07bd:$07be == $55:$aa
WarmBoot_Magic2 = $07be  ; second half of the warm-boot magic word; together with WarmBoot_Magic1 distinguishes warm restart from cold power-on
TrueScore_Lo = $07bf  ; lowest BCD digit of the actual (canonical) score. Game Genie 07BF:00 forces this to 0 every frame. The full true-score block is 6 BCD bytes at $07bf..$07c4, written by the score-add routines and copied to the HUD-display copy at $0427..$042b. Pinning all 6 to 0 (the 'True Score' cheat) makes the player rank as 0 score for high-score purposes
TrueScore_b1 = $07c0  ; second BCD digit of the true score (see TrueScore_Lo for full block notes)
TrueScore_b2 = $07c1  ; third BCD digit of the true score
TrueScore_b3 = $07c2  ; fourth BCD digit of the true score
TrueScore_b4 = $07c3  ; fifth BCD digit of the true score
TrueScore_Hi = $07c4  ; highest BCD digit of the true score
GameState_Active = $07c5  ; game-state flag: $00 at boot/title and after game-over (cleared at $c02a in init and $e195 in game-over alongside Lives_Tens/Ones); $ff during a life via Death_Sequence at $d7a3. Two title-screen consumers gate on it being nonzero: $b6f0 (skip the 2P menu row when cleared) and $bb1e (pick alternate HUD-tile sequence). Most consistent reading is 'a game session is in progress / has occurred since boot'
